</a></div><div style="clear:both;"></div></div><div><sup>Sponsored</sup></div></div><div class="cell show-for-medium medium-6" style="padding: 0.6rem;"><!-- 71161633/perfume_incontent_1/perfume_incontent_1 --><div data-fuse="22384494431"></div></div></div><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x grid-margin-y"><div class="cell small-6"><likes-rating :perfume_id="71888" chart="show" type-chart="small-chart" colors="retro"></likes-rating></div><div class="cell small-6"><seasons-rating :perfume_id="71888" chart="show" type-chart="small-chart" colors="retro"></seasons-rating></div><div class="small-12 medium-6 text-center" style="max-height: 50px"><div itemprop="aggregateRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/AggregateRating" itemscope><p class="info-note">Perfume rating&nbsp;<span itemprop="ratingValue">4.31</span>&nbsp;out of&nbsp;<span itemprop="bestRating">5</span> with&nbsp;<span itemprop="ratingCount" content="3013">3,013</span> votes<meta itemprop="reviewCount" content="331"/></p></div></div></div><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x grid-margin-y"><div class="cell small-12" itemprop="description" v-pre><p><b>Bad Boy Cobalt Parfum Electrique</b> by <b>Carolina Herrera</b> is a Woody Aromatic fragrance for men. This is a new fragrance. <b>Bad Boy Cobalt Parfum Electrique</b> was launched in 2022. The nose behind this fragrance is Domitille Michalon Bertier. Top notes are Lavender and Pink Pepper; middle notes are Plum and Geranium; base notes are Vetiver, Cedar, Truffle and Oak. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Following the global success of Bad Boy and Bad Boy Le Parfum, Carolina Herrera puts an electrifying twist on the dual nature of the modern man with Bad Boy Cobalt. This new men’s fragrance cracks open convention while exploring the diverse bonds of brotherhood, embodied in nature by the unapologetic strength found in cobalt and its powerfully pigmented blue. Working closely with Carolina A. Herrera, Creative Director of fragrances at Carolina Herrera, Perfumer Domitille Michalon Bertier delved into the depths of her imagination to develop this technically accomplished perfume. Together, they fused mineral sexiness and wild freshness for an energizing and contrasted new release, which is contained in a fresh cobalt blue conceptualization of the already iconic Bad Boy lightning bolt perfume bottle. Every fragrance has dominant notes that allow its message to be transmitted, giving it its soul and unique signature.</p>

<p>For Bad Boy Cobalt, the team chose to work with the incredible contrasts of the new “Magic Spark ELIXIR”, an ingredient that elegantly expresses the complementary contradictions of brotherhood, the nuance, and strength of a friendship between men. Just as cobalt dyes glass that particular shade of blue, this ELIXIR colors the fragrance from top to bottom with lively citrus accents, simultaneously producing intriguingly earthy undertones.</p>

<p>The Magic Spark ELIXIR blends pink pepper and geranium to create the fresher part of Bad Boy Cobalt. Pink pepper offers a distinctively fresh tone with aromatic and slightly floral suggestions, while geranium is a floral yet masculine note that was a prominent part of Carolina Herrera for Men, the first masculine fragrance from the house of Herrera, first launched in 1991. The mineral accents of a truffle accord are invigorated with the literal and metaphorical strength of oakwood, and infused with the masculinity of vetiver, together with the sexiness of cedarwood to create the hooking base of the fragrance.</p>

<p>“But it wasn’t just the symbolism of the lighting bolt that allowed my imagination to run wild,” says Domitille Michalon-Bertier. “Cobalt is found in the earth’s crust, and I found myself reflecting on lightning cracking Bad Boy Cobalt the ground open, revealing this chemical element together with the dense smells of the soil.” Oakwood, with its touch of smokiness, is a historical symbol of endurance, “beautifully representing the enduring strength within a band of brothers” to the creator of Bad Boy Cobalt.</p>

<p>Meanwhile, vetiver is a perennial plant, drawing its subtle fragrance from volcanic soil saturated with mineral salts, and is a classic ingredient of men’s perfumery. The essential oils of cedarwood has been extracted since ancient Egyptian times, here supplying a powerful dry and vibrating edge with additional clean and green facets.</p>

<p>At Carolina Herrera, vetiver has historically been a reference to exotic travel, to the Caribbean vistas of locations such as Haiti. Today, the House of Herrera creates this new fragrance using a vetiver sourced from Haiti, and is at the root of a program called Sourcing for Shared Value, which finds greener ways to grow and harvest this important ingredient while protecting the people who work the land by supporting with local education and infrastructure.</p>

<p>It’s a lengthy process to make sure that the vetiver used is the most beautiful, ethical, and greenest product for both the population and for the planet. In their distinctive ways, each fragrance in the Bad Boy family plays on the dual nature of the contemporary man, a concept that is reinforced and developed with Bad Boy Cobalt and its exploration of the bonds of brotherhood. Modern men are aware that there’s no strength without sensitivity, or power without compassion, so the short circuit of freshness in the top notes and the deep base notes of Bad Boy Cobalt are enhanced by a floral heart to the perfume.</p>

<p>Composed of clean aromatic lavender and juicy black plum, it evokes the emotional tenderness that’s at the center of the most durable of male friendships. The powerful contrasting nature of this masculine duality is enigmatically represented by the bottle, with its blue to transparent gradient. An exquisite reimagining of the emblematic lightning bolt from the Bad Boy universe, it shows us Bad Boy at his most elegant, inspired to be himself, and confident that anything is possible alongside his trusted and beloved friends.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a     <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
        <div class="cell destinationreview"></div>                    <div id="parent2351648" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2351648" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Zeptha0"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2325921"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2325921.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Zeptha0" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Rabanne/Invictus-Victory-Elixir-78575.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.78575.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Invictus Victory Elixir"title="Invictus Victory Elixir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2351648ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2351648" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2325921">Zeptha0</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-17">11/17/24 01:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I got this one about 6 months ago and overall i really like it. The performance is nothing special but it smells really nice when it does. One downside i can say is after wearing it for a while for me it started to smell sickening and made me almost gag every time i wore it. I stopped wearing it for a while and it got back to normal again.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2351648"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2351648#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2348891" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It has a fresh and pleasant aroma that’s incredibly likable and has definitely brought me some compliments. I started reaching for it more often than my other fragrances because of its unique appeal.<br />
<br />
However, the downside to Bad Boy Cobalt is its performance. The fragrance only lasts around 4-5 hours at best, and the sillage fades noticeably after the first hour. Compared to other fragrances with similar notes, it just doesn’t have the longevity or projection I’d hoped for. If it had better staying power, I’d probably buy it more often.<br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2329933" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Davidolool"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2165153"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Davidolool" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2329933ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2329933" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2165153">Davidolool</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-28">10/28/24 03:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A Carolina Herrera Bad Boy Cobalt mindig is kellett a gyüjteményemben és egy idő után úgy terveztem megveszem, de valami teljesen másra számítottam, mint amit kaptam. Egyszere szeretem és nem szeretem ezt a parfümöt, többet vártam tőle az áráért is és maga a Bad Boy családhoz képest, túl hypoltnak érzem. Nem egy túl férfias illat, mármint a fás illat jegyén kivül semmi férfiasság nincs benne. Az illatjegyéről egy rossz szót nem lehet elmondani fás, édes, kék illat finoman összehangolva, egy kellemes finom illat. Aki nem szereti a nagyon Óceános, vizi nyári illatokat ezt jobban fogja kedvelni a fás jegytől.<br />
<br />
Mikor alkalmas viselni:<br />
Igazából bármikor és szinte bárkinek, egy nagyon könnyen hordható parfüm, nem lesz sose sok, de nagyon kevés se, nyáron és tavaszzal érdemesebb hordani, de hidegebb időszakokban is lehet de kisebb erőségre kell számítani.<br />
<br />
Bókok:<br />
Ha szeretnél egy lány elött bevágodni segíteni fog ez az illatt nem találkoztam olyan nővel akinek ne tetszett volna az illat, nőknél bók mágnes. Férfiaknál megoszto a vélemény sokan egy gyenge túlárazott kölninek mondják.<br />
<br />
Teljesítmény:<br />
<br />
Talán ez az egyik legfájobb a parfümnél, én kifujás után 30 percig érzem a levegőbe, viszont más pedig érzi tovább, nagyon hamar hozzá szokik az orrom és ez zavar. Egyáltalán nincsen valami brutális zsilázsa, ilyen mérsékelt 1-2 óráíg, utána erősen gyengül 3-4 óra után pedig szinte csak bőrön lehet érezni. Összeségében 5-6 óra után eltünik, nekem gyenge a többi Designer és a Bad Boy családhozz képest is.<br />
<br />
Árérték, Végső itélett.<br />
Összegzésben egy jó, könnyen horható, kellemes illatt, egy nem jó teljesítménnyel. Szimplán zavar, hogy 130$/100ml-ért szinte alíg lehet rajtam érezni 2-3 óra után, csak ha közelebb kerülök valakivel. Végső szó, szeretem ezt az illattot, de ennyi pénzért sokkal jobbat is tudtam volna venni, túlárazott az értékhez képest.<br />
<br />
Ilatt: 8/10<br />
Szilázs: 6/10<br />
Hosszantartóság: 6/10<br />
Ár érték: 5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2329933"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2329933#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2329728" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; (it's my signature scent and I'm totally gatekeeping it. hahah)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2321119"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2321119#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2318584" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2318584" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Dracarys09"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2180431"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2180431.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Dracarys09" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2318584ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2318584" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2180431">Dracarys09</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-17">10/17/24 06:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Top note smells like blue raspberry sour patch kids</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2318584"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2318584#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2317187" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2317187" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TheDogfatherHTX"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1824841"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1824841.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TheDogfatherHTX" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Cactus-Garden-53946.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.53946.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Cactus Garden"title="Cactus Garden"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2317187ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2317187" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1824841">TheDogfatherHTX</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-16">10/16/24 00:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Carolina Herrera's Bad Boy may get a bit of hate in the fragcom, but there are some flankers in the line that get some love; Bad Boy Cobalt is one of them. A far departure from the rest of the line, Cobalt is the blue fragrance offering in the line. I've tried it on test strips at department stores and I'm always impressed when I get my nose on it. I finally committed to purchasing a full bottle so I can give it a proper test. Let's get into it;<br />
<br />
Scent:<br />
Opening is fruity, woody, and aromatic. The primary notes I get are plum, lavender, geranium, and vetiver. The strongest of the notes are the plum and lavender. The plum note is fruity uniquely fruity and sweet, albeit a bit synthetic. The lavender is soft and aromatic. It definitely sticks out, but doesn't wallop you in the face like some lavender notes can do. This is followed by the geranium and vetiver. The geranium brings a delicate floral note that's a bit green and rosy, while the vetiver rounds out the opening with a foundation of dusty woodiness. There's a bit more dustiness than typical with vetiver, and I'm assuming that's coming from the truffle note boosting that dusty and earthy accord. The dry down is aromatic, woody, and earthy. The primary notes I get are lavender, vetiver, cedar, and truffle. The strongest of the notes are the lavender and vetiver. The lavender and vetiver continue their same aromatic and woody accords from the opening. This is followed by the cedar and truffle. The cedar helps to amp up the woodiness in the dry down, while the truffle note has become a bit more noticeable and added even more earthy dustiness. There's just a touch of the fruitiness of the plum left, but it's faint. The dry down is nice, but the opening is much nicer in my opinion.<br />
<br />
Performance:<br />
Initial projection is nuclear and fills a room. Sillage matches that with a heavy scent trail. After a few hours the projection was still about arms length and the scent trail was still noticeable. Around hour 6 is when the fragrance became a skin scent.<br />
<br />
When to wear:<br />
In typical blue fragrance fashion, this would work anytime and anywhere. Warm weather or cool weather, formal or casual, at the office or on a date; it'll work for anything.<br />
<br />
Blind buy:<br />
If you like blue fragrances with some built in fruitiness (think YSL Y EDP or Invictus) this is a safe blind buy for you. Just keep that performance in mind if you prefer your fragrances to be beast mode.<br />
<br />
Final verdict:<br />
I would be lying if I said I wasn't a little disappointed in how Cobalt turned out. I was really hoping it would hold onto that plum note into the dry down to keep that sweet and fruity edge. Instead it leans more into the "blue-ness" with some dustiness and just a hint of the plum. If it had been able to hold onto the more interesting notes longer I think it could have been a home run. Performance isn't terrible at about 6 hours, but when we have fragrances like Y EDP that have a similar scent profile and monster performance Cobalt feels a bit lacking. In any case, I'm not upset about the purchase as I do enjoy it. I'll probably find myself reaching for this every once in a while, I'll just have to overspray a bit.<br />
<br />
Scent: 8/10<br />
Longevity: 6/10<br />
Sillage: 6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2317187"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2317187#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2316821" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Opening is sweet and magical. The sweetness is similar to other fragrances I own, and love, particularly Azzaro TMW and 1Million Parfum. I assume it's the ethyl maltol, but in this case it has a fruity nuance coming from the plum note. The truffle is subtle but helps to ground the layers with an earthy note that complements the woods. <br />
The dry down isn't as good - it resembles shower gel. The longevity also leaves much to be desired (6hrs). But for what it is, a blue fragrance for every occasion, it's fantastic and different enough to have an identity.<br />

<br />
The performance is lackluster and the smell isn't as alluring as other fragrances on the market. It's not a bad option, but I think you can go with way better fragrances. If you want a blue and sweet fragrance, I'd get the underrated Halloween Man Hero; if I wanted this same DNA but with better quality and performance, Invictus Platinum would be my choice</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; And personally, I don’t mind it.<br />
<br />
Blue, dynamic, fresh: imagine getting a freshly laundered pair of jeans. Did I say jeans? Yeah, jeans.<br />
<br />
This fragrance starts with a kick of lavender, and an hour later the geranium kicks in. But the drydown is one worth the money: woody, bright, and oh-so-blue.<br />
<br />
This fragrance runs the risk of smelling generic. No wonder people here are saying it smells similar to Invictus, Sauvage, Y and Hawas. But, if a gentleman that’s now matured and is wearing suits 5 out of 7 days in the week wants to relive a time he’d have 10 cents and a pair of jeans to his name, this is the one to spray on. But i gotta warn you, the woodiness in the dry-down is overstated by some of these reviews... for 4-5 hours this fragrance is very sweet &amp; fades quickly after that. If you like to overspray the only places i would recommend wearing this would be the gym or the club, but if you spray that thing less than most i'd say this could be a great daily scent for a sweet young boy. 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; This is because the bulk of the fragrance differs from the top note. The initial smell of this fragrance is like no other, the pink pepper, the plum, it’s absolutely intoxicating. This fades into a smell that I have heard been described as a blue jolly rancher and I agree fully, which isn’t a bad thing. But within 30 min this all fades to the base note of a subtle woody-ness. align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2208492"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2208492#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2205773" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2205773" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Buysblind"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/52178"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.52178.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Buysblind" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Hermes/H24-65147.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.65147.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="H24"title="H24"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2205773ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2205773" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/52178">Buysblind</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-02">07/02/24 08:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>THIS is what everybody’s been so excited about? Cobalt’s a pleasant “blue” fragrance in a tacky, though well-made bottle (the glass is solid, with an attractive ombré pattern and a good atomizer). There’s nothing particularly new or unique here, it recalls fragrances such as Invictus Legend, Dylan Blue, and perhaps a younger, more simplified Bleu de Chanel. It’s not bad though. Bad Boy Cobalt is fairly smooth, and it’s one of those fragrances where a lot of different notes seem to come together to create a singular scent—so there’s some depth and nuance to the fragrance itself. I find it more uplifting and polished than average, better than say, Dylan Blue or even the Y! EDP, but the genre itself has been  done to death at this point. Performance is solid all around, no problems there.  I guess what I was expecting here was more of a unique scent profile due to the plum note and “truffle” in the heart, but to be honest I think the note list is kind of baloney, which they more often than not are anyway. But I like it. It IS nice. Cobalt has a clean, airy quality that sits well and creates a nice sillage, and it avoids seeming harsh or overly chemical, as some “blue” fragrances do, and the woody element is done right, in the sense that it’s supporting the fragrance without interfering with it or overpowering the cool, breezy “plum” note up top. Similarly, if there is a citrus component (it doesn’t really seem like there is, but maybe a little bergamot), they did a nice job keeping it in check and preventing the fragrance from smelling sharp, which I don’t think would work well here. So overall, Bad Boy Cobalt has some nice things going for it and is a good offering within the genre (which I think we’re all a little tired of at this point). As for the hoopla around it….probably not necessary. But if you’re in the market for this sort of fragrance you could definitely do worse, and it’s worth giving Cobalt a look. Good for young folks, older guys are probably sick of this kind of scent by now. 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2205773"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2205773#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2205518" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Sillage: 4/10<br />
Price: 6/10<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1586079">Ghost13</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-02">05/02/24 14:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I bought this a few years back for my best friend after we smelled it in stores. She really likes wearing unisex or masculine fragrances compared to women’s fragrances due to more of the notes she enjoys being used in masc/unisex marketed perfumes. We both thought it smelled divine and even her father thought it was amazing. We both preferred it over the others in this line but the others are still very good in our opinion. It is very much an aromatic perfume with some sweet and woody accords. The plum in this is to die for and honestly if you want something that’s great for fall and winter and isn’t just a usual warm perfume I’d really recommend this. This is my bestie’s second favorite perfume just after her signature (d&amp;g light blue intense pour femme) and she has burned through not one but two 3.4oz bottles in the span of two years. I would just say go a little lighter in the summer. Oh and one final note, this will linger in the air. I was once driving her after she put some on in our house and even for hours after I dropped her off to work, I could still smell it in my car (my seats are leather if that is important). <br />
Overall I really love it especially compared to most designer mens perfumes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2143626"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2143626#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2142156" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2010907">Fragnautical</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-04">04/04/24 10:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>an electric SHOCK straight into the veins like sticking a fork into an electrical socket.<br />
<br />
despite its tacky bottle design, this frag doesn't joke. opening of sweet plums and geranium bathes the fraghead in ecstasy, recalling memories of strolling through a sunny park or through a landry soap isle.<br />
<br />
drydown eases into a nice woody, earthly scent of truffles, cedarwood, oak and vetiver. a sweetness perfect for the average, testosterone filled male. fun fact: truffles contain androstenol, a key component in testosterone, which helps wild boars hunt for them and find them easily in the forest. the saliva of a boar also contains androstenol. yummy! those chest hairs will grow in no time!<br />
<br />
longevity can vary. i get a good 4 to 5 hours from this scent easily in hot kitchens which i work. the sillage varies too. either way it'll depend on the user's skin chemistry.<br />
<br />
footnote edit: the atomizer is KILLER. nice, wide sprays and distance. one or two on neck usually is enough.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2114221"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2114221#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2108454" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; To sum up my thoughts, this fragrance smells like the color blue in all the best ways possible. The opening hits you with a punch of Lavender and surprisingly fresh plum mixed with a little spice from the pink pepper. The dry down holds its own and the earthier notes are much more present about 2-3 hours after applying. This scent feels very sophisticated and also very versatile. It’s a warmer weather fragrance but it can be worn anytime. As for longevity it’s decent, nothing nuclear and not bad at all, I have smelled it on my skin about 8 hours after applying. Overall great fragrance and I do recommend. Bad Boy Cobalt Parfum Electrique is your secret weapon for turning heads wherever you go. Created by Carolina Herrera, this fragrance is all about blending freshness with depth, giving you an irresistible charm.<br />
<br />
Picture this: a sleek cobalt-blue bottle that practically screams sophistication. It's like holding confidence in your hand. And the scent? It's a journey. Imagine zesty mandarin and bergamot kicking things off, waking up your senses. Then comes the heart of the fragrance, with hints of sage and rosemary adding layers of complexity. Finally, settle into the base notes—tonka bean, musk, and amber—leaving a warm and memorable trail behind you.<br />
<br />
Whether you're heading to a meeting or hitting the town, this fragrance is your wingman. It's not just a scent; it's your ticket to being remembered. So, why wait? 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2091137"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2091137#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2090231" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I am unsure why so many people rated this as a Summer fragrance, as it is far too heavy for use in high heat. 6 sprays lasts me several hours, and I can still catch small whiffs of it 8 hours later. <br />
<br />

Definitely a very energizing opening if you couldn’t tell by the bottle of design! The dark fruit notes really shine through here in a very potent opening. <br />
<br />
As the scent begins to dry down, a peppery, yet still dark fruit, sweet scent begins to form without losing its potency. And some soapiness/ clean notes also starts to take over a little bit here, but nothing that overpowers.  <br />
<br />
When the scent settles in more wood and earthiness come through with still that sweetness from the fruit <br />
<br />
<br />
For the price I think it’s a goodbye, but definitely would recommend testing it out on skin first as it can be a very potent smell even after a few hours<br />
<br />

Synthetic plum has a weird aftersmell. But if it smells good on your skin I wouldn't mind smelling it once in a while. very unique, but it copies some DNA from other fragrances. <br />
<br />
Good unique, I like, but not in love.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2073477"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2073477#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2070066" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; But a worthwhile addition if you like fruity/juicy  frags that don't take themselves too seriously.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2046989"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2046989#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2045075" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2028987"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2028987#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2028426" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2028426" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="nicholassua"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/11042"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.11042.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="nicholassua" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Valentino/Valentino-Uomo-19558.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.19558.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Valentino Uomo"title="Valentino Uomo"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2028426ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2028426" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/11042">nicholassua</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-12">01/12/24 01:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Le Parfum and Cobalt smells different from the OG<br />
I love the OG, and I hate Le Parfum and Cobalt.. <br />
<br />
Cobalt = Invictus Platinum</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2028426"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2028426#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2027745" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2027745" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="CorgRage"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1305327"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1305327.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="CorgRage" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2027745ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2027745" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1305327">CorgRage</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-11">01/11/24 09:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>TLDR; <br />
Love this on my boyfriend. A unique fresh fragrance for those who have liked this “genre” in the past. Men with complementary body chemistry may find the truffle note grounds this in a very sexy and earthy way, playing up their more natural, “masculine” musk. That’s a rare find and peculiar accomplishment for a fresh fragrance. /end<br />
<br />
I’m the girlfriend who bought this as a gift, and the designated “scent lover.” I’ve tried to introduce this world to my partner. He prefers to have one fragrance, with maybe one or two other options for different weather or dates. I knew he liked freshies, he’s used invictus in the past. To me, this one was perfect option in that realm without being too cookie cutter (he loved it as well.)<br />
<br />
As you’d expect, this is one of those “sweet” men’s fresh fragrances that has a really definable profile and line up. I staunchly disagree that it lacks its own character or place. <br />
<br />
You can’t go wrong with a lavender and pink pepper opening, and the geranium in this is played up. There’s a bite to it. It’s not really aromatic or green, but almost minty and somehow tart. It still holds steadfast to that common quality of these freshies, the plum note they created here bringing that sweetness. It makes me think of if you were to eat the skin of the plum first, getting little nibbles of the actual fruit while grazing on the much more tart and green portion. I also never get tired of a cedar and vetiver base. To me disliking a more common base in a perfume like saying you’re tired of a delicious flavor-enhancing spice because it’s used in too many dishes.   <br />
<br />
Fun fact, truffle smells like (and contains) Androstenol, the by-product of testosterone. It’s responsible for a man’s natural “musk” scent, so by creating a truffle base it’s likely they were trying to emulate a more lived-in scent that smells like a damn man. It worked, its smells so so good on my partner and mixes with his natural scent (and even sweat) perfectly. It’s really his perfect every day scent. I bet that aspect really varies based on the individual, but the truffle addition grounds this fragrance perfectly and adds an earthy element. <br />
<br />
I didn’t love the idea of the lightening bolt bottle. Ironically, purchasing the largest 5.1 oz changed my mind. Very well made and heavy, and the glass fade is a nice touch. Depending on your decor style, this could be a nice “eclectic” display bottle. <br />
<br />
Unimportant side note: If I were to be completely honest, I think there’s a level of snobbery surrounding men’s fragrances that’s kind of sad and is reflected in reviews here. I won’t begrudge them, I feel like in some ways there’s a lack of perceived masculinity to enjoying fragrances, so to separate from that people may feel drawn to invoke a sense of luxury, success, or exclusivity (which often means snubbing some great stuff because it was created by a main stream brand they dislike, even subconsciously.) For the sake of fragrances, this is great! If you put this in a plain, blank bottle and THEN had people test it, I’d be interested to see if their opinions differ. <br />
<br />
If you don’t like it, that’s fine. We all know our brains are literally wired to intake scent differently. I think it’s a real gem, and it will be my partners signature for a very long time.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2027745"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2027745#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2026964" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2026964" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jqwalls"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1778223"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1778223.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jqwalls" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Fragrance-One/Office-For-Men-55166.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.55166.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Office For Men"title="Office For Men"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2026964ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2026964" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1778223">Jqwalls</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-10">01/10/24 15:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The plum and truffle notes are what makes this fragrance stand out from the crowd. It is addictive. Very sweet but also slightly earthy. It is just different enough to make it smell special and be that much more enjoyable to wear than something more common and boring like other mass appealing men’s frags like Bleu de Chanel or cool water. Performance is similar to Bleu and others in the same price range although not even close to the performance of sauvage edt. I sampled this fragrance for a couple weeks and went back and forth on whether or not it was worth buying at retail price but I was able to get it for $90 on eBay and at that price I feel like it is absolutely worth it. I really like this one and I’m glad I got it. Easily could be a daily signature scent. 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2026964"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2026964#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2026236" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2025114"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2025114#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2024096" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2024096" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Glue"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1896091"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1896091.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Glue" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Givenchy/L-Interdit-Absolu-95831.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.95831.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="L'Interdit Absolu"title="L'Interdit Absolu"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2024096ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2024096" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1896091">Glue</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-08">01/08/24 01:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>What I mostly get here is the lavender and a lot of sweetness. Very generic and boring to my taste, someone already mentioned below that it smells like when you enter a perfume store and you can smell a mix of everything that was sprayed there in the air. <br />
You can wear it all year round but I wouldn't really wear it in hot summer days as it's too sweet. The projection and longevity are ok but at this price point could be better.<br />
<br />
I suppose it's a good every day scent if you don't want to stand out or just wear something to the office but I think there are some better choices out there. I would rather go for Bleu de Chanel EDP, YSL La Nuit de L'Homme Bleu Électrique, YSL Y EDP or even much cheaper Rasasi Hawas if I felt like wearing a blue fragrance.<br />
<br />
Based on the tacky bottle and the name I think it's mostly targeted at boys and young men below 21 but the cheapest 100ml bottle I could find is around 90 eur so I'm not sure about that marketing.<br />
<br />
It's a no from me as it's boring but if you're looking for a generic everyday scent, this will do the job.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2024096"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2024096#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2020430" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2020430" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="V1CT"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1547801"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1547801.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="V1CT" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2020430ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2020430" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1547801">V1CT</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-04">01/04/24 15:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>In Carolina Herrera's Bad Boy Cobalt Parfum Electrique, an aromatic lavender is the main note that I smell throughout this fragrance. With the first spray, it opens with a great burst of airy lavender that is more fresh than sweet compared to other scents that use lavender such as Y EDP Intense or Sauvage. The lavender lingers for quite a long time and it keeps the scent staying bright and relaxing to smell.<br />
<br />
As Bad Boy Cobalt dries down past the first 10 minutes or so, the plum note emerges, making the fragrance smell very sweet. I understand that there are many types of sweet in the world of fragrance, but this plum note smells like a candy and fruity sweetness. This makes the fragrance smell very youthful, playful, and mass-appealing that won't choke others out in the high heat as compared to other fragrances with sweet notes. The notes of lavender and plum go so well together to make this scent very elegant and tickles the nose if sprayed correctly.<br />
<br />
I don't seem to smell truffle at all in Bad Boy Cobalt, but perhaps I don't know what to look for in the base. After about 2 or 3 hours, Bad Boy Cobalt leaves a soft, woody scent that I would not describe as overly masculine compared to other wood bases, but still retains its sweetness that it's kept throughout the entire scent. Cedarwood makes itself known, but not so much the oak.<br />
<br />
In terms of longevity, Bad Boy Cobalt top notes last around 10 or 20 minutes, then drys down to the heart and lingers for 3 to 4 hours. I still smell the scent after a full day of running errands of about 6 to 7 hours, and the scent lasts much longer when sprayed on clothes. I tend to spray 3 sprays on my neck, 2 behind each ear, 1 behind my head, and 2 on each arm crease. This scent smells very good in the air, but does not project as much in the time that I've worn it; this might change in the hotter seasons when the climate is warmer and the scent can work its magic. Definitely a great choice for spring and summer, and I'll be wearing this to my 2024 summer trip to Vietnam.<br />
<br />
 TL;DR - Bad Boy Cobalt is a sweet, fresh, youthful scent that is a great choice for younger men during the spring, summer, and fall months. The lively lavender and the juicy plum notes make the scent very mass-appealing and easy on the nose. Longevity is average, about 6 to 7 hours, and projection is about a foot or two in the first hour. Very pretty bottle with a fire hose of an atomizer, Bad Boy Cobalt is a great addition to any collection!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="2020430"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=2020430#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2020253" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1988317" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RayCashhhh"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1295740"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1295740.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RayCashhhh" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Imaginary-Authors/Falling-Into-The-Sea-16549.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.16549.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Falling Into The Sea"title="Falling Into The Sea"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1988317ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1988317" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1295740">RayCashhhh</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-29">11/29/23 12:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If Bleu de Chanel is the king of blue fragrances, then Bad Boy Cobalt is the heir to the throne. BdC Parfum is one of my favorite fragrances ever, an easy to reach for scent that got the job done no matter the occasion. However, I have preferred Cobalt a lot more recently, as I think it's even easier to wear. Bleu de Chanel has gotten a "mature" rep from some, and I do think it's spot on (although not necessarily a bad thing). Bad Boy Cobalt has a more youthful vibe in my opinion, replacing the woodiness of BdC with a delectable plum note. Maybe it's just me, but I find Cobalt to be different from the plethora of blue fragrances on the market, although it's certainly a "shower gel" scent. I think the fresh and fruity scent profile is hard to dislike, and while the longevity isn't spectacular, it's adequate for most wearings. Cobalt is different from the others in the Bad Boy lineage; it does have sweetness via the ripe plum, but it's easily the freshest and most versatile. This and the Extreme are probably my favorite designer releases of the decade, and for good reason. 9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="1988317"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=1988317#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1977817" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1977817" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JusttheFactsMan"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733487"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1733487.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JusttheFactsMan" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Azzaro/Wanted-by-Night-49144.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.49144.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Wanted by Night"title="Wanted by Night"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1977817ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1977817" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733487">JusttheFactsMan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-16">11/16/23 04:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>#412 in my "Tour de Fragrance"<br />
<br />
Bought this as a sprayette to try it out. Enough scent to wear it for a few days. I really like it. But I've never disliked any Carolina Herrera frag I've tried. Likability is never the issue. They are always great scents that are inoffensive and attractive. Potency is always the issue for me. They are all moderate performers at best, and I only want more potency because I truly, truly like the scents and would like them to make it to lunch AND beyond, but they never do. So I feel like the Bad Boys are overpriced and it dampens my enthusiasm for the scents. I truly hate the lightning bolt bottles, even more than I hate the Moschino bear, the Paco Rabanne robot, and Reyane door bolt bottles, but I will live with them to get the good stuff they contain. I don't think they create anything but buyer hesitancy and annoyance, but I'll live with them. Someone walks into your bathroom and see these toys on the shelf, doesn't reflect well on your maturity or taste.<br />
<br />
This frag makes it to lunch, barely, i.e. three-four hours tops. So while the longevity is not awful for a blue, it is not impressive, and I would wish for better. I think it's a legit year rounder. I think it's very versatile and most anyone who smells it will like it. It's a blue/green. i.e. blue notes with an aromatic green grass note that really freshens and sharpens the overall impression. It won't drive anyone out of the car, the elevator or the office. In fact, of all the Bad Boy scents I believe this is the best one for office wear, though the least soft and cuddly. The other Bad Boys are probably better date scents, Cobalt is better for day wear. But still, I think the Bad Boys are overpriced, especially as the older 212 line is now reasonable for what you get. I recently paid $60 for 212 Wins and felt great about it. I would not feel great paying $95-$125 for this fragrance. So I'm ordering a tester at $80. Still not a good buy, but not toothache painful.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="1977817"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=1977817#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1976051" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1951409" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Siprian85"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1477503"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1477503.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Siprian85" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Rabanne/Million-Gold-95641.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.95641.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Million Gold"title="Million Gold"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1951409ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1951409" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1477503">Siprian85</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-13">10/13/23 23:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The  Bad Boy Cobalt EDP Electrique by Carolina<br />
Herrera (CH), is an<br />
Woody Aromatic fragrance for men. The nose behind<br />
this fragrance is Domitille Michalon Bertier.<br />
The notes for this fragrance are as follows:<br />
Top notes: Pink Pepper and Lavender<br />
Middle notes: Plum and Geranium<br />
Base notes : Truffle, Vetiver and Cedar<br />
Personally, this fragrance does not resemble anything<br />
like the Bad Boy EDT or the Bad Boy Le parfum. In fact,<br />
it's much better in both design and scent wise. The removed the tacky sprayer which was so uncomfortable to use to a gold top atomiser. The first impression I get is this Aromatic alluring scent and it slowly dries down to a mature with a hint of sweetness in the mid, until it finally rests and projects Vetiver and Cedar notes within an arm length.<br />
Overall Rating: 8,5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="1951409"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=1951409#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1946692" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I'm not crazy about designer scents but, this is certainly quite impressive.<br />
<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="1861420"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=1861420#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1856787" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The black plum is such a seductive sent and very prominent. The black plum note stays throughout the entire life of the fragrance, giving up a lot of room for the woods after a while.<br />
<br />
Works well for any time of the year, day or night. The very sweet opening quickly turns into a nice "blue" woody scent with that black plum lingering in the background. This is a very versatile fragrance with a nice sillage and long lasting too (I go 4-8 sprays depending on temperature, and i get good projection for all of 8+ hours).<br />
<br />
Unfortunately, i got long covid and my lungs aren't healing properly. This is one of the Many fragrances that badly effect my ability to breath due to long covid, and i therefor had to get rid of. I miss it. It was my daily work scent for almost 6 months. And i love it.<br />
<br />
Personal score: 9/10. It Does smell very synthetic. But it is a CH fragrance, so i can't take points for that. I love and miss it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="1856787"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=1856787#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1854111" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
