<br />
People are complaining about the opening, but I do love a good spicy spin to knock my nose into a near-sneezing state 🤣 It's zingy, but smells like it has bergamot (which isn't listed here), it's not merely a spicy experience, there's some freshness. <br />
<br />
It has a juicy blue quality to it, and I think "plum" is a fair note to call it. It's refreshing, and not unlike a blue raspberry drink 😋 <br />
<br />
Despite this being a little unisex in it's opening-mid stage, it does manage to dry down into a more masculine base fragrance. It's a little funky and oak-y, and like it a lot...but not necessarily on myself. I don't smell true truffle or vetiver, but it's a bit dirt-tastic! I'm testing my husband's sample, and look forward to him wearing this! It's decent designer release, and while I don't find it crazy attractive, I think it's fun and it has a certain appeal.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="1560678"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=1560678#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1988317" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1988317" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RayCashhhh"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1295740"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1295740.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RayCashhhh" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Imaginary-Authors/Falling-Into-The-Sea-16549.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.16549.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Falling Into The Sea"title="Falling Into The Sea"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1988317ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1988317" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1295740">RayCashhhh</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-29">11/29/23 12:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If Bleu de Chanel is the king of blue fragrances, then Bad Boy Cobalt is the heir to the throne. BdC Parfum is one of my favorite fragrances ever, an easy to reach for scent that got the job done no matter the occasion. However, I have preferred Cobalt a lot more recently, as I think it's even easier to wear. Bleu de Chanel has gotten a "mature" rep from some, and I do think it's spot on (although not necessarily a bad thing). Bad Boy Cobalt has a more youthful vibe in my opinion, replacing the woodiness of BdC with a delectable plum note. Maybe it's just me, but I find Cobalt to be different from the plethora of blue fragrances on the market, although it's certainly a "shower gel" scent. I think the fresh and fruity scent profile is hard to dislike, and while the longevity isn't spectacular, it's adequate for most wearings. Cobalt is different from the others in the Bad Boy lineage; it does have sweetness via the ripe plum, but it's easily the freshest and most versatile. This and the Extreme are probably my favorite designer releases of the decade, and for good reason. 9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="71888"comment_id="1988317"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Parfum-Electrique-71888.html?ccid=1988317#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="71888" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
